Top 64 Decklists
================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on October 30, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/olle_rade_author.jpg)
By Olle Rade











Warsaw was full of sweet decks, and to bring you as many of them as possible, here are the players who finished from 33rd to 64th place.

#####
